# Add OTLP Exporter Support for Tracing

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Language:** Go
**Difficulty:** hard

## Problem

Flipt currently only supports Jaeger and Zipkin as tracing exporters, limiting observability integration options for teams using OpenTelemetry collectors or other OTLP-compatible backends. Users cannot export trace data using the OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP), which is becoming the standard for telemetry data exchange in cloud-native environments. This forces teams to either use intermediate conversion tools or stick with legacy tracing backends.

## Reproduction

1. Enable tracing in Flipt configuration
2. Attempt to set `tracing.exporter: otlp` in configuration
3. Start Flipt service and observe configuration validation errors
4. Note that only `jaeger` and `zipkin` are accepted as valid exporter values

## Key Components

- Tracing exporter initialization — where Jaeger/Zipkin exporters are created
- Configuration schema — where valid exporter values are defined and validated
- Exporter factory/selection logic

## Task

1. Add `otlp` as a supported tracing exporter alongside `jaeger` and `zipkin`
2. When `otlp` is selected, allow configuration of an endpoint (default: `localhost:4317`)
3. Maintain `jaeger` as the default exporter when no exporter is specified
4. Ensure configuration validation accepts all three exporter values without errors
5. Run existing tests to ensure no regressions

## Success Criteria

- Setting `tracing.exporter: otlp` starts the service without validation errors
- OTLP exporter connects to the configured endpoint (or default `localhost:4317`)
- Default behavior (Jaeger) is unchanged when exporter is not specified
- Existing Jaeger and Zipkin configurations continue to work
- All existing tests pass

     3→import (

     5→	"sync"

     7→	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
     8→	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
     9→)
    10→
    11→var (
    12→	traceExpOnce sync.Once
    13→	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
    14→	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
    15→	traceExpErr  error
    16→)
    17→
    18→// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
    19→// Supports OTLP
    20→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
    21→	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
    22→		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    23→		if traceExpErr != nil {
    24→			return
    25→		}
    26→
    27→		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    28→			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    29→		}
    30→	})
    31→
    32→	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
    33→}
    34→

    43→	for k, v := range m {
    44→		switch t := v.(type) {
    45→		case map[string]any:
    46→			adapt(t)
    47→		case time.Duration:
    48→			m[k] = t.String()
    49→		}
    50→	}
    51→}

     1→package tracing
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→	"sync"
     6→
     7→	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
     8→	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
     9→)
    10→
    11→var (
    12→	traceExpOnce sync.Once
    13→	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
    14→	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
    15→	traceExpErr  error
    16→)
    17→
    18→// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
    19→// Supports OTLP
    20→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
    21→	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
    22→		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    23→		if traceExpErr != nil {
    24→			return
    25→		}
    26→
    27→		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    28→			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    29→		}
    30→	})
    31→
    32→	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
    33→}
    34→

Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the Flipt tracing architecture. Let me compile a detailed summary report:

## Flipt Tracing Architecture Summary

Based on my thorough exploration of the Flipt codebase, here's a detailed summary of how tracing is currently configured and initialized:

### 1. TracingConfig Structure Definition

**File:** `/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`

```go
type TracingConfig struct {
	Enabled bool `json:"enabled" mapstructure:"enabled" yaml:"enabled"`
}

func (c *TracingConfig) setDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error {
	v.SetDefault("tracing.enabled", false)
	return nil
}
```

The TracingConfig is minimal and contains only a single boolean field `Enabled` that defaults to `false`. This is the only explicit configuration option for tracing at the config level.

### 2. GetExporter Implementation

**File:** `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`

```go
func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
		if traceExpErr != nil {
			return
		}

		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
		}
	})

	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
}
```

The GetExporter function:
- Uses a sync.Once pattern to ensure the exporter is only created once (singleton pattern)
- Relies entirely on OpenTelemetry's `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` to automatically detect and configure the exporter
- Returns the SpanExporter, a shutdown function, and any error
- **Comments in code state "Supports OTLP"** - indicating OTLP is the only supported export format

**File:** `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` (lines 179-203)

```go
// Initialize

     1→package tracing

     9→)
    10→
    11→var (
    12→	traceExpOnce sync.Once
    13→	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
    14→	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
    15→	traceExpErr  error
    16→)
    17→
    18→// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
    19→// Supports OTLP
    20→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
    21→	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
    22→		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    23→		if traceExpErr != nil {
    24→			return
    25→		}
    26→
    27→		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    28→			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    29→		}
    30→	})
    31→
    32→	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
    33→}

## Detailed Summary: Flipt Metrics Exporters Pattern

Based on my exploration of the Flipt codebase, here's a comprehensive analysis of how metrics exporters are configured and implemented. This serves as the template for implementing tracing exporters.

---

### 1. Configuration Structure (Type-Safe with Enum/Constants)

**File:** `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go`

```go
type MetricsExporter string

const (
	MetricsPrometheus MetricsExporter = "prometheus"
	MetricsOTLP       MetricsExporter = "otlp"
)

type MetricsConfig struct {
	Enabled  bool            `json:"enabled" mapstructure:"enabled" yaml:"enabled"`
	Exporter MetricsExporter `json:"exporter,omitempty" mapstructure:"exporter" yaml:"exporter,omitempty"`
}

func (c *MetricsConfig) setDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error {
	v.SetDefault("metrics.enabled", true)
	v.SetDefault("metrics.exporter", MetricsPrometheus)
	return nil
}
```

**Key Pattern Elements:**
- Defines a string type alias `MetricsExporter` for type safety
- Uses const with the type alias to define allowed values
- Implements the `defaulter` interface with `setDefaults()` method
- YAML/JSON serialization with `mapstructure` tags for config file support
- Viper integration for defaults and environment variable override support

---

    26→		logExp, logExpErr = autoexport.NewLogExporter(ctx, autoexport.WithFallbackLogExporter(fallbackExporterFactory))
    27→		if logExpErr != nil {
    28→			return
    29→		}
    30→
    31→		logExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    32→			return logExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    33→		}
    34→	})
    35→
    36→	return logExp, logExpFunc, logExpErr
    37→}
    38→
    39→// noopLogExporter is an implementation of logsdk.Exporter that performs no operations.

**Core Dependencies:**
- `go.opentelemetry.io/otel v1.40.0` - Core OTel library
- `go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk v1.40.0` - SDK for traces
- `go.opentelemetry.io/otel/trace v1.40.0` - Trace API
- `go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport v0.65.0` - Auto-exporter detection

**Specific Exporter Packages (Already Imported):**

- `go.opentelemetry.io/otel/exporters/otlp/otlptrace/otlptracehttp v1.40.0` - OTLP HTTP transport
- `go.opentelemetry.io/otel/exporters/prometheus v0.62.0` - Prometheus (for metrics, not traces)

**Instrumentation & Propagation:**
- `go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/instrumentation/google.golang.org/grpc/otelgrpc v0.65.0` - gRPC instrumentation

- `go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/propagators/autoprop v0.65.0` - Auto-propagator detection

## Summary

I've analyzed the Flipt codebase extensively and created a detailed implementation plan for adding OTLP exporter support. The plan follows Flipt's established patterns for configurable exporters (mirroring the metrics exporter pattern).

**Key Implementation Points:**

1. **Extend TracingConfig** with an `Exporter` field and constants for `jaeger`, `zipkin`, and `otlp`
2. **Update CUE schema** to validate exporter values
3. **Refactor GetExporter()** to accept config and use switch-based exporter selection
4. **Set Jaeger as default** when not specified (maintaining backward compatibility)
5. **Configure OTLP endpoints** with default `localhost:4317`
6. **Add comprehensive tests** following the metrics testing pattern

The implementation plan is documented in `/logs/agent/sessions/plans/drifting-baking-journal.md` and is ready for implementation.

    21→// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
    22→// Supports OTLP, Jaeger, and Zipkin exporters.
    23→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context, cfg *config.TracingConfig) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
    24→	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
    25→		switch cfg.Exporter {
    26→		case config.TracingOTLP:
    27→			// Configure OTLP endpoint from config
    28→			if cfg.Endpoint != "" {
    29→				os.Setenv("OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT", cfg.Endpoint)
    30→			}
    31→			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    32→			if traceExpErr != nil {
    33→				return
    34→			}
    35→
    36→			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    37→				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    38→			}
    39→
    40→		case config.TracingJaeger:
    41→			// Configure Jaeger via environment
    42→			os.Setenv("OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER", "jaeger")
    43→			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    44→			if traceExpErr != nil {
    45→				return
    46→			}
    47→
    48→			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    49→				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    50→			}
    51→
    52→		case config.TracingZipkin:
    53→			// Configure Zipkin via environment

... (truncated)

    50→	}

     1→# Implementation Plan: Add OTLP Exporter Support for Tracing
     2→
     3→## Context
     4→
     5→Flipt currently uses OpenTelemetry's autoexport feature for tracing, which automatically detects exporters based on environment variables. The `TracingConfig` only has an `Enabled` boolean field and provides no explicit configuration for exporter type or endpoints.
     6→
     7→The goal is to add explicit tracing exporter configuration support (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) in the configuration file, allowing users to:
     8→1. Specify which exporter to use in the config file (not just environment variables)
     9→2. Configure exporter-specific endpoints with sensible defaults
    10→3. Make tracing exporters configurable like metrics exporters already are
    11→4. Maintain backward compatibility with environment variable configuration
    12→
    13→## Key Findings from Codebase Exploration
    14→
    15→### Current Architecture
    16→- **Tracing Config:** Only has `Enabled` boolean (`/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`)
    17→- **Exporter Creation:** Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` which auto-detects based on env vars
    18→- **Pattern Reference:** Metrics exporters use a switch-statement pattern with type-safe configuration
    19→- **Dependencies:** OTLP (gRPC and HTTP) packages already imported; Jaeger/Zipkin not imported yet
    20→- **Initialization:** Occurs in `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` lines 181-203
    21→
    22→### Metrics Pattern (to be replicated for tracing)
    23→Location: `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go` and `/workspace/internal/otel/metrics/metrics.go`
    24→
    25→1. **Config Structure:** Type alias `MetricsExporter` with constants
    26→2. **Exporter Constants:** `MetricsPrometheus` and `MetricsOTLP`
    27→3. **Swit
... (truncated)

     - **Zipkin**: Sets `OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER=zipkin` for autodetection

   - Proper error handling for unsupported exporters

values and builds up a set of environment variables\n// compatible with viper's expectations for automatic env capability.\nfunc readYAMLIntoEnv(t *testing.T, path string) [][2]string {\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\tconfigFile, err := os.ReadFile(path)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar config map[any]any\n\terr = yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, &config)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\treturn getEnvVars(\"flipt\", config)\n}\n\nfunc getEnvVars(prefix string, v map[any]any) (vals [][2]string) {\nOUTER:\n\tfor key, value := range v {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), v)...)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tbuilder := strings.Builder{}\n\t\t\tfor i, s := range v {\n\t\t\t\tswitch s := s.(type) {\n\t\t\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\t\t\t// descend into slices of objects\n\t\t\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), s)...)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue OUTER\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", s))\n\t\t\t\t\tif i < len(v)-1 {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteByte(' ')\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tbuilder.String(),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", value),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn vals\n}\n\nfunc TestMarshalYAML(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct {\n\t\tname    string\n\t\tpath    string\n\t\twantErr error\n\t\tcfg     func() *Config\n\t}{\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tname: {\n\tconfigType := reflect.TypeFor[Config]()\n\tconfigTags := getStructTags(configType)\n\n\tfor k, v := range camelCaseMatchers {\n\t\tstrcase.ConfigureAcronym(k, v)\n\t}\n\n\t// Validate the struct tags for the Config struct.\n\t// recursively validate the struct tags for all sub-structs.\n\tvalidateStructTags(t, configTags, configType)\n}\n\nfunc validateStructTags(t *testing.T, tags map[string]map[string]string, tType reflect.Type) {\n\ttName := tType.Name()\n\tfor fieldName, fieldTags := range tags {\n\t\tfieldType, ok := tType.FieldByName(fieldName)\n\t\trequire.True(t, ok, \"field %s not found in type %s\", fieldName, tName)\n\n\t\t// Validate the `json` struct tag.\n\t\tjsonTag, ok := fieldTags[\"json\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isCamelCase(jsonTag), \"json tag for field '%s.%s' should be camelCase but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, jsonTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Validate the `mapstructure` struct tag.\n\t\tmapstructureTag, ok := fieldTags[\"mapstructure\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isSnakeCase(mapstructureTag), \"mapstructure tag for field '%s.%s' should be snake_case but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, mapstructureTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Validate the `yaml` struct tag.\n\t\tyamlTag, ok := fieldTags[\"yaml\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isSnakeCase(yamlTag), \"yaml tag for field '%s.%s' should be snake_case but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, yamlTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// recursively validate the struct tags for all sub-structs.\n\t\tif fieldType.Type.Kind() == reflect.Struct {\n\t\t\tvalidateStructTags(t, getStructTags(fieldType.Type), fieldType.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc isCamelCase(s string) bool {\n\treturn s == strcase.ToLowerCamel(s)\n}\n\nfunc isSnakeCase(s string) bool {\n\t// Special case: sigv4 follows the naming convention\n\tif s == \"sigv4\" {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\treturn s == strcase.ToSnake(s)\n}\n\nfunc getStructTags(t reflect.Type) map[string]map[string]string {\n\ttags := make(map[string]map[string]string)\n\n\tfor field := range t.Fields() {\n\t\t// Get the field name.\n\t\tfieldName := field.Name\n\n\t\t// Get the field {\n\t\t\t\tfieldTags[tag] = \"skip\"\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tvalues := strings.Split(tagValue, \",\")\n\t\t\tif len(values) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\ttagValue = values[0]\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif tagValue != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tfieldTags[tag] = tagValue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttags[fieldName] = fieldTags\n\t}\n\n\treturn tags\n}\n\nfunc TestLicenseConfig_validate(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct secrets.Manager) error {\n\tswitch v.Kind() {\n\tcase reflect.String:\n\t\tif v.CanSet() {\n\t\t\tstr := v.String()\n\t\t\t// Check if this is a secret reference using the regex\n\t\t\tif secretReference.MatchString(str) {\n\t\t\t\t// Extract the reference: ${secret:reference} -> reference\n\t\t\t\treference := secretReference.ReplaceAllString(str, `$1`)\n\n\t\t\t\t// Parse the reference format: either \"key\" or \"provider:key\"\n\t\t\t\tparts := strings.Split(reference, \":\")\n\n\t\t\t\tvar secretRef secrets.Reference\n\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\tcase len(parts) == 1:\n\t\t\t\t\t// Simple format: \"key-name\" - use default provider\n\t\t\t\t\tsecretRef = secrets.Reference{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tProvider: \"\", // Use default provider\n\t\t\t\t\t\tPath:     parts[0],\n\t\t\t\t\t\tKey:      parts[0],\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcase len(parts) == 2:\n\t\t\t\t\t// Simple format: \"provider:key\"\n\t\t\t\t\tsecretRef = secrets.Reference{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tProvider: 'provider:key'\", reference)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// Resolve the secret\n\t\t\t\tsecretValue, err := secretsManager.GetSecretValue(ctx, secretRef)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase reflect.Pointer:\n\t\tif !v.IsNil() {\n\t\t\tif err := walkConfigForSecrets(ctx, v.Elem(), secretsManager); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase reflect.Map:\n\t\tfor _, key := range v.MapKeys() {\n\t\t\tvalue := v.MapIndex(key)\n\t\t\tif value.Kind() == reflect.Interface && !value.IsNil() {\n\t\t\t\tvalue = value.Elem()\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Map values from MapIndex are not addressable, so we need to create\n\t\t\t// an addressable copy, resolve secrets in it, and set it back\n\t\t\tif value.Kind() == reflect.Struct {\n\t\t\t\t// Create a new addressable copy of the struct\n\t\t\t\tnewValue := reflect.New(value.Type()).Elem()\n\t\t\t\tnewValue.Set(value)\n\n\t\t\t\tif err := walkConfigForSecrets(ctx, newValue, secretsManager); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// Set the modified value back into the map\n\t\t\t\tv.SetMapIndex(key, newValue)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tif err := walkConfigForSecrets(ctx, value, secretsManager); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n",

No extraordinary resources\n// are consumed, or goroutines initialized until a SpanProcessor is registered.\ntracingProvider := tracesdk.NewTracerProvider(\n\ttracesdk.WithResource(otelResource),\n)\n\nserver.onShutdown(tracingProvider.Shutdown)\n\nif cfg.Tracing.Enabled {\n\texp, traceExpShutdown, err := tracing.GetExporter(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"creating tracing exporter: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tserver.onShutdown(traceExpShutdown)\n\n\ttracingProcessor := tracesdk.NewBatchSpanProcessor(exp)\n\tserver.onShutdown(tracingProcessor.Shutdown)\n\n\ttracingProvider.RegisterSpanProcessor(tracingProcessor)\n\tlogger.Debug(\"otel tracing enabled\")\n}\n\nopentelemetry.SetTracerProvider(tracingProvider)\nopentelemetry.SetTextMapPropagator(autoprop.NewTextMapPropagator())\n```\n\nKey initialization points:\n- TracerProvider is **always created** with an OTel Resource containing Flipt service name and version\n- The SpanExporter is **only initialized if `cfg.Tracing.Enabled` is true**\n- Uses `BatchSpanProcessor` to batch spans for efficient export\n- Text map propagator is set to `autoprop.NewTextMapPropagator()` (auto-detecting propagator format)\n- gRPC instrumentation is enabled conditionally (lines 401-405):\n  ```go\n  if cfg.Tracing.Enabled {\n      statsHandler := otelgrpc.NewServerHandler()\n      grpcOpts = append(grpcOpts, grpc.StatsHandler(statsHandler))\n      ipch = ipch.WithServerStatsHandler(statsHandler)\n  }\n  ```\n\n### 4. Environment Variables and Configuration Options\n\n**Primary Configuration:**\n- **`FLIPT_TRACING_ENABLED`** or `tracing.enabled` in config file (boolean, defaults to `false`)\n  - Defined in CUE schema at `/workspace/config/flipt.schema.cue` (lines 321-323)\n\n**Automatic Detection via autoexport (Environment-driven):**\n\nThe autoexport package automatically detects and configures exporters based on **OTEL environment variables**:\n\n1. **OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER** - Specifies the trace exporter type\n2. **OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT** - OTLP collector endpoint\n3. **OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_PROTOCOL** - Protocol (grpc or http/protobuf)\n4. **OTEL_RESOURCE_ATTRIBUTES** - Service resource attributes\n5. **OTEL_LOGS_EXPORTER** - For log exporting (used in main.go line 291)\n\n**Special handling in main.go:**\n```go\nif os.Getenv(\"OTEL_LOGS_EXPORTER\") != \"\" {\n    // Initialize log exporter and provider\n}\n```\n\n### 5. autoexport.NewSpanExporter Capabilities\n\n**Files:** `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`, `/workspace/internal/otel/metrics/metrics.go`, `/workspace/internal/otel/logs/logs.go`\n\nThe `go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport` package provides three functions:\n\n1. **`autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)`** (traces/tracing.go)\n   - Creates span exporters (for distributed tracing)\n   - No configuration object needed\n   \n2. **`autoexport.NewMetricReader(ctx)`** (metrics/metrics.go)\n   - Creates metric readers/exporters\n   - Used only for OTLP metrics (line 151 in metrics.go):\n   ```go\n   case config.MetricsOTLP:\n       metricExp, metricExpErr = autoexport.NewMetricReader(ctx)\n   ```\n   - Metrics also support explicit Prometheus exporter\n\n3. **`autoexport.NewLogExporter(ctx, autoexport.WithFallbackLogExporter(...))`** (logs/logs.go)\n   - Creates log exporters\n   - Includes fallback mechanism to `noopLogExporter` if OTLP logging not configured\n\n### 6. OTel Resource Configuration\n\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/otel/resource.go`\n\n```go\nfunc NewResource(ctx context.Context, fliptVersion string) (*resource.Resource, error) {\n\tresourceOnce.Do(func() {\n\t\trsrc, resourceErr = resource.New(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tresource.WithSchemaURL(semconv.SchemaURL),\n\t\t\tresource.WithAttributes(\n\t\t\t\tsemconv.ServiceName(\"flipt\"),\n\t\t\t\tsemconv.ServiceVersion(fliptVersion),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t\tresource.WithFromEnv(),      // Reads OTEL_RESOURCE_ATTRIBUTES\n\t\t\tresource.WithTelemetrySDK(),\n\t\t\tresource.WithContainer(),\n\t\t\tresource.WithHost(),\n\t\t\tresource.WithProcessRuntimeVersion(),\n\t\t\tresource.WithProcessRuntimeName(),\n\t\t\tresource.WithProcessRuntimeDescription(),\n\t\t)\n\t})\n\treturn rsrc, resourceErr\n}\n```\n\nThe resource includes:\n- Service name: `\"flipt\"`\n- Service version: from build info\n- Automatic environment-based attributes via `WithFromEnv()`\n- Container, host, and runtime metadata\n\n### 7. Current Architecture Summary\n\n**Exporter Selection Flow:**\n```\nconfig.Tracing.Enabled = true\n    \u2193\ntracing.GetExporter(ctx)\n    \u2193\nautoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)\n    \u2193\nChecks OTEL environment variables:\n  - OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER (defaults to \"otlp\")\n  - OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT\n  - OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_PROTOCOL\n    \u2193\nReturns appropriate SDK exporter (OTLP is the default/only supported)\n```\n\n**Limitations:**\n- No file-based exporter configuration in current implementation\n- Only supports OTLP-based exporters through autoexport\n- Exporter type is environment-variable driven, not config-file driven\n- No explicit exporter selection in TracingConfig struct\n\n### Key Files and Line References\n\n| File | Lines | Purpose |\n|------|-------|---------|\n| `/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go` | 1-21 | TracingConfig definition |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go` | 1-34 | GetExporter implementation |\n| `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` | 179-203, 401-405 | Tracing initialization |\n| `/workspace/config/flipt.schema.cue` | 321-323 | Schema validation |\n| `/workspace/cmd/flipt/main.go` | 291-323 | Logs exporter setup |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/resource.go` | 1-40 | Resource creation |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/metrics/metrics.go` | 140-166 | Metrics exporter (for comparison) |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/logs/logs.go` | 1-58 | Logs exporter (for comparison) |\n\nThis architecture demonstrates a clean separation between configuration (minimal TracingConfig) and exporter initialization (via autoexport), with environment variables driving the actual exporter selection and endpoint configuration.",

{
  "content": "# Implementation Plan: Add OTLP Exporter Support for Tracing\n\n## Context\n\nFlipt currently uses OpenTelemetry's autoexport feature for tracing, which automatically detects exporters based on environment variables. The `TracingConfig` only has an `Enabled` boolean field and provides no explicit configuration for exporter type or endpoints.\n\nThe goal is to add explicit tracing exporter configuration support (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) in the configuration file, allowing users to:\n1. Specify which exporter to use in the config file (not just environment variables)\n2. Configure exporter-specific endpoints with sensible defaults\n3. Make tracing exporters configurable like metrics exporters already are\n4. Maintain backward compatibility with environment variable configuration\n\n## Key Findings from Codebase Exploration\n\n### Current Architecture\n- **Tracing Config:** Only has `Enabled` boolean (`/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`)\n- **Exporter Creation:** Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` which auto-detects based on env vars\n- **Pattern Reference:** Metrics exporters use a switch-statement pattern with type-safe configuration\n- **Dependencies:** OTLP (gRPC and HTTP) packages already imported; Jaeger/Zipkin not imported yet\n- **Initialization:** Occurs in `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` lines 181-203\n\n### Metrics Pattern (to be replicated for tracing)\nLocation: `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go` and `/workspace/internal/otel/metrics/metrics.go`\n\n1. **Config Structure:** Type alias `MetricsExporter` with constants\n2. **Exporter Constants:** `MetricsPrometheus` and `MetricsOTLP`\n3. **Switch Logic:** In `GetExporter()`, switch on exporter type to create appropriate instance\n4. **Error Handling:** Unsupported exporter returns formatted error\n5. **Shutdown Functions:** Optional shutdown function for cleanup\n6. **Default:** Set via `setDefaults()` viper calls\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Overview\nImplement tracing exporters following the established metrics pattern, focusing on OTLP support with placeholders for future Jaeger/Zipkin additions.\n\n### Changes Required\n\n#### 1. **Update TracingConfig Structure**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`\n\nAdd type-safe exporter configuration mirroring metrics pattern:\n- Create `TracingExporter` string type alias\n- Define constants: `TracingJaeger`, `TracingZipkin`, `TracingOTLP`\n- Add `Exporter` field to `TracingConfig`\n- Add optional `Endpoint` field for OTLP configuration\n- Update `setDefaults()` to set default exporter to Jaeger and OTLP endpoint to `localhost:4317`\n\n#### 2. **Update CUE Schema**\n**File:** `/workspace/config/flipt.schema.cue` (lines 321-323)\n\nExtend the `#tracing` schema definition to include:\n```cue\n#tracing: {\n\tenabled?:  bool | *false\n\texporter?: *\"jaeger\" | \"zipkin\" | \"otlp\"\n\tendpoint?: string | *\"localhost:4317\"  // Only used for OTLP\n}\n```\n\n#### 3. **Refactor GetExporter Implementation**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`\n\n- Modify signature to accept `*config.TracingConfig` parameter (like metrics does)\n- Add switch statement based on `cfg.Exporter` value\n- For each exporter type:\n  - **OTLP:** Set `OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT` env var from config, then call `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()`\n  - **Jaeger:** Set `OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER=jaeger` env var, then call `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()`\n  - **Zipkin:** Set `OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER=zipkin` env var, then call `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()`\n- Keep singleton pattern with sync.Once\n- Add default case for unsupported exporters with error message\n\n#### 4. **Update Default Configuration**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/config/config.go` (Default() function around line 640)\n\nUpdate `Tracing` configuration in Default() from:\n```go\nTracing: TracingConfig{\n\tEnabled: false,\n},\n```\n\nTo:\n```go\nTracing: TracingConfig{\n\tEnabled:  false,\n\tExporter: TracingJaeger,\n\tEndpoint: \"localhost:4317\",  // Default OTLP endpoint\n},\n```\n\n#### 5. **Update Tracing Initialization**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` (lines 187-189)\n\nUpdate the exporter initialization call from:\n```go\nexp, traceExpShutdown, err := tracing.GetExporter(ctx)\n```\n\nTo:\n```go\nexp, traceExpShutdown, err := tracing.GetExporter(ctx, &cfg.Tracing)\n```\n\n#### 6. **Add Logging**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` (around line 199)\n\nAfter successful exporter setup, add:\n```go\nlogger.Debug(\"otel tracing exporter configured\", zap.String(\"exporter\", string(cfg.Tracing.Exporter)))\n```\n\n#### 7. **Create Tests**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go` (new file)\n\nImplement table-driven tests following metrics pattern:\n- Test OTLP exporter creation with default endpoint\n- Test Jaeger exporter creation\n- Test Zipkin exporter creation\n- Test unsupported exporter error handling\n- Test singleton pattern (reset between tests)\n- Test shutdown function behavior\n\n### Implementation Notes\n\n**Backward Compatibility:**\n- Environment variables still work (OpenTelemetry standard)\n- Config file settings take precedence via env var override in GetExporter()\n- No breaking changes to existing configuration\n\n**Exporter Selection Priority:**\n1. Config file `tracing.exporter` value (if tracing enabled)\n2. OTLP endpoint from config or environment variable\n3. Environment variables (OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER, OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT)\n4. Default to Jaeger if nothing specified\n\n**Endpoint Configuration:**\n- OTLP: Configurable endpoint with default `localhost:4317`\n- Jaeger: Uses autoexport (endpoint via OTEL_EXPORTER_JAEGER_ENDPOINT env var)\n- Zipkin: Uses autoexport (endpoint via OTEL_EXPORTER_ZIPKIN_URL env var)\n\n## Critical Files to Modify\n\n| File | Changes | Lines/Sections |\n|------|---------|---|\n| `/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go` | Add Exporter type and constants, update setDefaults() | Complete rewrite |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go` | Add config parameter, implement switch logic | Complete rewrite of GetExporter() |\n| `/workspace/config/flipt.schema.cue` | Extend #tracing schema | Lines 321-323 |\n| `/workspace/internal/config/config.go` | Update Default() function | Around line 640 |\n| `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` | Update GetExporter() call | Line 188 |\n| `/workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go` | Create new test file | New file |\n\n## Verification Plan\n\n### Testing\n1. Run existing tracing tests to ensure no regressions\n2. Run new tracing exporter tests to verify all exporters\n3. Run schema validation tests to ensure CUE schema is valid\n4. Run full config tests to ensure configuration parsing works\n\n### Manual Verification\n1. Set `tracing.enabled: true` and `tracing.exporter: otlp` with custom endpoint\n2. Verify service starts without validation errors\n3. Test that each exporter type (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) can be selected\n4. Verify default behavior (jaeger) when not specified\n5. Ensure backward compatibility with OTEL environment variables\n6. Verify configuration validation rejects unsupported exporter values\n\n### Expected Behavior After Implementation\n- Users can configure tracing exporter in config file\n- OTLP exporter connects to configured endpoint (default localhost:4317)\n- Jaeger is default when no exporter specified\n- Zipkin and Jaeger remain functional\n- All existing tests pass\n- Configuration schema validation includes all three exporters\n",

vars to obtain the potential keys which populate\n// the unbound map keys.\nfunc bind(env, prefixes []string, next string, fn func([]string)) {\n\t// given the previous entry is non-existent or not the wildcard\n\tif len(prefixes) < 1 || prefixes[len(prefixes)-1] != wildcard {\n\t\tfn(appendIfNotEmpty(prefixes, next))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// drop the wildcard and derive all the possible keys from\n\t// existing environment variables.\n\tp := make([]string, len(prefixes)-1)\n\tcopy(p, prefixes[:len(prefixes)-1])\n\n\tvar (\n\t\t// makezero linter doesn't take note of subsequent copy\n\t\t// nolint https://github.com/ashanbrown/makezero/issues/12\n\t\tprefix = strings.ToUpper(strings.Join(append(p, \"\"), \"_\"))\n\t\tkeys   = strippedKeys(env, prefix, strings.ToUpper(next))\n\t)\n\n\tfor _, key := range keys {\n\t\tfn(appendIfNotEmpty(p, strings.ToLower(key), next))\n\t}\n}\n\n// strippedKeys returns a set of keys derived from a list of env var keys.\n// It starts by filtering and stripping each key with a matching prefix.\n// Given a child delimiter string is supplied it also trims the delimeter string\n// and any remaining characters after this suffix.\n//\n// e.g strippedKeys([\"A_B_C_D\", \"A_B_F_D\", \"A_B_E_D_G\"], \"A_B\", \"D\")\n// returns [\"c\", \"f\", \"e\"]\n//\n// It's purpose is to extract the parts of env vars which are likely\n// keys in an arbitrary map type.\nfunc strippedKeys(envs []string, prefix, delim string) (keys []string) {\n\tfor _, env := range envs {\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(env, prefix) {\n\t\t\tenv = env[len(prefix):]\n\t\t\tif env == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif delim == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, env)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// cut the string on the child key and take the left hand component\n\t\t\tif left, _, ok := strings.Cut(env, \"_\"+delim); ok {\n\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, left)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\n// getFliptEnvs returns all environment variables which have FLIPT_\n// as a prefix. It also strips this prefix before appending them to the\n// resulting set.\nfunc getFliptEnvs() (envs []string) {\n\tconst prefix = \"FLIPT_\"\n\tfor _, e := range os.Environ() {\n\t\tkey, _, ok := strings.Cut(e, \"=\")\n\t\tif ok && strings.HasPrefix(key, prefix) {\n\t\t\t// strip FLIPT_ off env vars for convenience\n\t\t\tenvs = append(envs, key[len(prefix):])\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn envs\n}\n\nfunc (c *Config) validate() error {\n\tif c.Version != \"\" {\n\t\tif strings.TrimSpace(c.Version) != Version {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid version: %s\", c.Version)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif c.Authorization.Required && !c.Authentication.Required {\n\t\treturn errString(\"authorization\", \"requires authentication to also be required\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Check that environment storage references exist in storage config\n\tfor envName, env := range c.Environments {\n\t\tif env.Storage == \"\" {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif _, exists := c.Storage[env.Storage]; !exists {\n\t\t\treturn errString(\"environments\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%q references undefined storage %q\", envName, env.Storage))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Validate templates {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n}\n\n// stringToEnumHookFunc returns a DecodeHookFunc that converts strings to a target enum\nfunc stringToEnumHookFunc[T constraints.Integer](mappings map[string]T) mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n\treturn func(\n\t\tf reflect.Type,\n\t\tt reflect.Type,\n\t\tdata any,\n\t) (any, error) {\n\t\tif f.Kind() != reflect.String {\n\t\t\treturn data, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif t != reflect.TypeOf(T(0)) {\n\t\t\treturn data, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tenum := mappings[data.(string)]\n\n\t\treturn enum, nil\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc experimentalFieldSkipHookFunc(types ...reflect.Type) mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n\treturn func(\n\t\tf reflect.Type,\n\t\tt reflect.Type,\n\t\tdata any,\n\t) (any, error) {\n\t\tif len(types) == 0 ${env:VAR} - environment variables\n// - ${secret:key} - secret references (marked as unresolved placeholders)\nfunc stringToReferenceHookFunc() mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n\treturn func(\n\t\tf The `TracingConfig` only has an `Enabled` boolean field and provides no explicit configuration for exporter type or endpoints.\n\nThe goal is to add explicit tracing exporter configuration support (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) in the configuration file, allowing users to:\n1. Specify which exporter to use in the config file (not just environment variables)\n2. Configure exporter-specific endpoints with sensible defaults\n3. Make tracing exporters configurable like metrics exporters already are\n4. Maintain backward compatibility with environment variable configuration\n\n## Key Findings from Codebase Exploration\n\n### Current Architecture\n- **Tracing Config:** Only has `Enabled` boolean (`/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`)\n- **Exporter Creation:** Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` which auto-detects based on env vars\n- **Pattern Reference:** Metrics exporters use a switch-statement pattern with type-safe configuration\n- **Dependencies:** OTLP (gRPC and HTTP) packages already imported; Jaeger/Zipkin not imported yet\n- **Initialization:** Occurs in `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` lines 181-203\n\n### Metrics Pattern (to be replicated for tracing)\nLocation: `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go` and `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()`\n  - **Zipkin:** Set `OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER=zipkin` env var, then call `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()`\n- Keep singleton pattern with sync.Once\n- Add default case for unsupported exporters with error message\n\n#### 4. **Update Default Configuration**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/config/config.go` (Default() function around line 640)\n\nUpdate `Tracing` configuration in Default() from:\n```go\nTracing: TracingConfig{\n\tEnabled: false,\n},\n```\n\nTo:\n```go\nTracing: TracingConfig{\n\tEnabled:  false,\n\tExporter: TracingJaeger,\n\tEndpoint: \"localhost:4317\",  // Default OTLP endpoint\n},\n```\n\n#### 5. **Update Tracing Initialization**\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` (lines 187-189)\n\nUpdate the exporter initialization tests)\n- Test shutdown function behavior\n\n### Implementation Notes\n\n**Backward Compatibility:**\n- Environment variables still work (OpenTelemetry standard)\n- Config file settings take The `TracingConfig` only has an `Enabled` boolean field and provides no explicit configuration for exporter type or endpoints.\n\nThe goal is to add explicit tracing exporter configuration support (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) in the configuration file, allowing users to:\n1. Specify which exporter to use in the config file (not just environment variables)\n2. Configure exporter-specific endpoints with sensible defaults\n3. Make tracing exporters configurable like metrics exporters already are\n4. (`/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`)\n- **Exporter Creation:** Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` which auto-detects based on env vars\n- **Pattern Reference:** Metrics exporters use a switch-statement pattern with type-safe configuration\n- **Dependencies:** OTLP (gRPC and HTTP) packages already imported; Jaeger/Zipkin not imported yet\n- **Initialization:** Occurs in `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` lines 181-203\n\n### Metrics Pattern (to be replicated for tracing)\nLocation: `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go` and 1. WRITE /logs/agent/sessions/plans/drifting-baking-journal.md
# Implementation Plan: Add OTLP Exporter Support for Tracing

## Context

Flipt currently uses OpenTelemetry's autoexport feature for tracing, which automatically detects exporters based on environment variables. The `TracingConfig` only has an `Enabled` boolean field and provides no explicit configuration for exporter type or endpoints.

The goal is to add explicit tracing exporter configuration support (otlp, jaeger, zipkin) in the configuration file, allowing users to:
1. Specify which exporter to use in the config file (not just environment variables)
2. Configure exporter-specific endpoints with sensible defaults
3. Make tracing exporters configurable like metrics exporters already are
4. Maintain backward compatibility with environment variable configuration

## Key Findings from Codebase Exploration

### Current Architecture
- **Tracing Config:** Only has `Enabled` boolean (`/workspace/internal/config/tracing.go`)
- **Exporter Creation:** Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter()` which auto-detects based on env vars
- **Pattern Reference:** Metrics exporters use a switch-statement pattern with type-safe configuration
- **Dependencies:** OTLP (gRPC and HTTP) packages already imported; Jaeger/Zipkin not imported yet
- **Initialization:** Occurs in `/workspace/internal/cmd/grpc.go` lines 181-203

### Metrics Pattern (to be replicated for tracing)
Location: `/workspace/internal/config/metrics.go` and `/workspace/internal/otel/metrics/metrics.go`

1. **Config Structure:** Type alias `MetricsExporter` with constants

package config

import (
	"github.com/spf13/viper"
)

var (
	_ defaulter = (*TracingConfig)(nil)
)

type TracingExporter string

const (
	TracingJaeger TracingExporter = "jaeger"
	TracingZipkin TracingExporter = "zipkin"
	TracingOTLP   TracingExporter = "otlp"
)

// TracingConfig contains fields, which configure tracing telemetry
// output destinations.
type TracingConfig struct {
	Enabled  bool            `json:"enabled" mapstructure:"enabled" yaml:"enabled"`
	Exporter TracingExporter `json:"exporter,omitempty" mapstructure:"exporter" yaml:"exporter,omitempty"`
	Endpoint string          `json:"endpoint,omitempty" mapstructure:"endpoint" yaml:"endpoint,omitempty"`
}

func (c *TracingConfig) setDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error {
	v.SetDefault("tracing.enabled", false)
	v.SetDefault("tracing.exporter", TracingJaeger)
	v.SetDefault("tracing.endpoint", "localhost:4317")
	return nil
}

5. EDIT /workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go
Before
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"sync"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
)

var (
	traceExpOnce sync.Once
	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
	traceExpErr  error
)

// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
// Supports OTLP
func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
		if traceExpErr != nil {
			return
		}

		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
		}
	})

	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
}
After
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"sync"

	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/config"
	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
)

var (
	traceExpOnce sync.Once
	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
	traceExpErr  error
)

// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
// Supports OTLP, Jaeger, and Zipkin exporters.
func GetExporter(ctx context.Context, cfg *config.TracingConfig) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
		switch cfg.Exporter {
		case config.TracingOTLP:
			// Configure OTLP endpoint from config
			if cfg.Endpoint != "" {
				os.Setenv("OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT", cfg.Endpoint)
			}
			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		case config.TracingJaeger:
			// Configure Jaeger via environment
			os.Setenv("OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER", "jaeger")
			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		case config.TracingZipkin:
			// Configure Zipkin via environment
			os.Setenv("OTEL_TRACES_EXPORTER", "zipkin")
			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		default:
			traceExpErr = fmt.Errorf("unsupported tracing exporter: %s", cfg.Exporter)
			return
		}
	})

	return traceExp, tra
... (truncated)

		exp, traceExpShutdown, err := tracing.GetExporter(ctx, &cfg.Tracing)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating tracing exporter: %w", err)
		}

		server.onShutdown(traceExpShutdown)

		tracingProcessor := tracesdk.NewBatchSpanProcessor(exp)
		server.onShutdown(tracingProcessor.Shutdown)

		tracingProvider.RegisterSpanProcessor(tracingProcessor)
		logger.Debug("otel tracing exporter configured", zap.String("exporter", string(cfg.Tracing.Exporter)))

7. WRITE /workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"errors"
	"sync"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/config"
)

func TestGetExporter(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name    string
		cfg     *config.TracingConfig
		wantErr error
	}{
		{
			name: "jaeger exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingJaeger,
			},
		},
		{
			name: "zipkin exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingZipkin,
			},
		},
		{
			name: "otlp exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,
				Endpoint: "localhost:4317",
			},
		},
		{
			name: "otlp exporter with custom endpoint",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,
				Endpoint: "otel-collector:4317",
			},
		},
		{
			name: "unsupported exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: "unsupported",
			},
			wantErr: errors.New("unsupported tracing exporter: unsupported"),
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			// Reset the singleton state for each test
			traceExpOnce = sync.Once{}
			traceExp = nil
			traceExpFunc = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
			traceExpErr = nil

			exp, expFunc, err := GetExporter(t.Context(), tt.cfg)
			if tt.wantErr != nil {
				require.EqualError(t, err, tt.wantErr.Error())
				assert.Nil(t, exp, "expected nil exporter when error occurs")
				return
			}

			require.NoError(t, err)
			assert.NotNil(t, exp)
			assert.NotNil(t, expFunc)

			t.Cleanup(func() {
				err := expFunc(context.Background())
				assert.NoError(t, err)
			})
		})
	}
}
